# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
prefix sum = 4
cumulative sum of previous frequencies
occurences of 4(x) + sum of frequencies of previous elements(y)
 ^NmBITy2s

I need frequencies of 4 at the time of output ^Pmmje20l

x + y - x ^B2A74Eca

in the index of sorted array set value to : current element
where index = frequency of current element - 1  ^fk6bXs4B
